victim of variant Creutzfeldt-Jakob Disease (vCJD), noted for unprecedented survival rate of a decade with the disease</li></ul>\n</div>\n<h2><span class="mw-headline" id="Education">Education</span><span class="mw-editsection"><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">[</span><a href="/w/index.php?title=Belfast&amp;action=edit&amp;section=29" title="Edit section: Education">edit</a><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">]</span></span></h2>\n<div role="note" class="hatnote navigation-not-searchable">See also: <a href="/wiki/List_of_primary_schools_in_Belfast" class="mw-redirect" title="List of primary schools in Belfast">List of primary schools in Belfast</a>, <a href="/wiki/List_of_secondary_schools_in_Belfast" title="List of secondary schools in Belfast">List of secondary schools in Belfast</a>, and <a href="/wiki/List_of_grammar_schools_in_Belfast" class="mw-redirect" title="List of grammar schools in Belfast">List of grammar schools in Belfast</a></div>\n<p>Belfast has two universities. <a href="/wiki/Queen%27s_University_Belfast" title="Queen&#39;s University Belfast">Queen\'s University Belfast</a> was founded in 1845 and is a member of the <a href="/wiki/Russell_Group" title="Russell Group">Russell Group</a>, an association of 24 leading research-intensive universities in the UK.<sup id="cite_ref-224" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-224">&#91;221&#93;</a></sup> It is one of the largest universities in the UK with 25,231 undergraduate and postgraduate students spread over 250 buildings, 120 of which are listed as being of architectural merit.<sup id="cite_ref-225" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-225">&#91;222&#93;</a></sup>\n</p><p><a href="/wiki/Ulster_University" title="Ulster University">Ulster University</a>, created in its current form in 1984, is a multi-centre university with a campus in the <a href="/wiki/Cathedral_Quarter,_Belfast" title="Cathedral Quarter, Belfast">Cathedral Quarter</a> of Belfast. The Belfast campus has a specific focus on Art and Design and Architecture, and is currently undergoing major redevelopment. The <a href="/wiki/Jordanstown" title="Jordanstown">Jordanstown</a> campus, just seven miles (11&#160;km) from Belfast city centre concentrates on engineering, health and social science. The <a href="/wiki/Coleraine" title="Coleraine">Coleraine</a> campus, about 55&#160;mi (89&#160;km) from Belfast city centre concentrates on a broad range of subjects. Course provision is broad \xe2\x80\x93 biomedical sciences, environmental science and geography, psychology, business, the humanities and languages, film and journalism, travel and tourism, teacher training and computing are among the campus strengths. The <a href="/wiki/Magee_College" title="Magee College">Magee</a> campus, about 70&#160;mi (113&#160;km) from Belfast city centre has many teaching strengths; including business, computing, creative technologies, nursing, Irish language and literature, social sciences, law, psychology, peace and conflict studies and the performing arts. The <a href="/wiki/Conflict_Archive_on_the_Internet" title="Conflict Archive on the Internet">Conflict Archive on the Internet</a> (CAIN) Web Service receives funding from both universities and is a rich source of information and source material on the Troubles as well as society and politics in Northern Ireland.<sup id="cite_ref-226" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-226">&#91;223&#93;</a></sup>\n</p><p><a href="/wiki/Belfast_Metropolitan_College" title="Belfast Metropolitan College">Belfast Metropolitan College</a> is a large <a href="/wiki/Further_education" title="Further education">further education</a> college with three main campuses around the city, including several smaller buildings. Formerly known as Belfast Institute of Further and Higher Education, it specialises in <a href="/wiki/Vocational_education" title="Vocational education">vocational education</a>. The college has over 53,000 students enrolled on full-time and part-time courses, making it one of the largest further education colleges in the UK and the largest in the island of Ireland.<sup id="cite_ref-227" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-227">&#91;224&#93;</a></sup>\n</p><p>The <a href="/wiki/Belfast_Education_and_Library_Board" class="mw-redirect" title="Belfast Education and Library Board">Belfast Education and Library Board</a> was established in 1973 as the local council responsible for education, youth and library services within the city.<sup id="cite_ref-228" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-228">&#91;225&#93;</a></sup> In 2006, this board became part of the <a href="/wiki/Education_Authority" title="Education Authority">Education Authority</a> for Northern Ireland. There are 184 primary, secondary and <a href="/wiki/Grammar_school" title="Grammar school">grammar</a> schools in the city.<sup id="cite_ref-229" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-229">&#91;226&#93;</a></sup>\n</p>\n<h2><span class="mw-headline" id="Tourism">Tourism</span><span class="mw-editsection"><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">[</span><a href="/w/index.php?title=Belfast&amp;action=edit&amp;section=30" title="Edit section: Tourism">edit</a><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">]</span></span></h2>\n<div class="thumb tright"><div class="thumbinner" style="width:222px;"><a href="/wiki/File:Titanic_Belfast_side_view.jpg" class="image"><img alt="" src="//upload.wikimedia.org/wikipedia/commons/thumb/4/44/Titanic_Belfast_side_view.jpg/220px-Titanic_Belfast_side_view.jpg" decoding="async" width="220" height="162" class="thumbimage" srcset="//upload.wikimedia.org/wikipedia/commons/thumb/4/44/Titanic_Belfast_side_view.jpg/330px-Titanic_Belfast_side_view.jpg 1.5x, //upload.wikimedia.org/wikipedia/commons/thumb/4/44/Titanic_Belfast_side_view.jpg/440px-Titanic_Belfast_side_view.jpg 2x" data-file-width="2340" data-file-height="1728" /></a>  <div class="thumbcaption"><div class="magnify"><a href="/wiki/File:Titanic_Belfast_side_view.jpg" class="internal" title="Enlarge"></a></div><a href="/wiki/Titanic_Belfast" title="Titanic Belfast">Titanic Belfast</a>, devoted to the Belfast-built <a href="/wiki/RMS_Titanic" class="mw-redirect" title="RMS Titanic">RMS <i>Titanic</i></a>, opened in 2012</div></div></div>\n<p>Belfast is one of the most visited cities in the UK,<sup id="cite_ref-230" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-230">&#91;227&#93;</a></sup> and the second most visited on the island of Ireland.<sup id="cite_ref-231" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-231">&#91;228&#93;</a></sup> In 2008, 7.1&#160;million tourists visited the city.<sup id="cite_ref-232" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-232">&#91;229&#93;</a></sup> Numerous popular tour bus companies and boat tours run there throughout the year, including tours based on the popular series <a href="/wiki/Game_of_Thrones" title="Game of Thrones">Game of Thrones</a>, which has had various filming locations around Northern Ireland.<sup id="cite_ref-233" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-233">&#91;230&#93;</a></sup>\n</p><p><a href="/wiki/Frommer%27s" title="Frommer&#39;s">Frommer\'s</a>, the American travel guidebook series, listed Belfast as the only United Kingdom destination in its <i>Top 12 Destinations to Visit</i> in 2009. The other listed destinations were <a href="/wiki/Berlin,_Germany" class="mw-redirect" title="Berlin, Germany">Berlin</a> (Germany), <a href="/wiki/Cambodia" title="Cambodia">Cambodia</a>, <a href="/wiki/Cape_Town" title="Cape Town">Cape Town</a> (South Africa), <a href="/wiki/Cartagena,_Colombia" title="Cartagena, Colombia">Cartagena</a> (Colombia), <a href="/wiki/Istanbul" title="Istanbul">Istanbul</a> (Turkey), the <a href="/wiki/Lassen_Volcanic_National_Park" title="Lassen Volcanic National Park">Lassen Volcanic National Park</a> (US), <a href="/wiki/Saqqara" title="Saqqara">Saqqara</a> (Egypt), the <a href="/wiki/Selma_To_Montgomery_National_Historic_Trail" class="mw-redirect" title="Selma To Montgomery National Historic Trail">Selma To Montgomery National Historic Trail</a> (US), <a href="/wiki/Waiheke_Island" title="Waiheke Island">Waiheke Island</a> (New Zealand), Washington, D.C. (US), and <a href="/wiki/Waterton_Lakes_National_Park" title="Waterton Lakes National Park">Waterton Lakes National Park</a> (Canada).<sup id="cite_ref-234" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-234">&#91;231&#93;</a></sup>\n</p><p>The Belfast City Council is currently investing into the complete redevelopment of the Titanic Quarter, which is planned to consist of apartments, hotels, and a riverside entertainment district. A major visitor attraction, <a href="/wiki/Titanic_Belfast" title="Titanic Belfast">Titanic Belfast</a> is a monument to Belfast\'s maritime heritage on the site of the former Harland &amp; Wolff shipyard, opened on 31 March 2012. It features a criss-cross of escalators and suspended walkways and nine high-tech galleries.<sup id="cite_ref-235" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-235">&#91;232&#93;</a></sup> They also hope to invest in a new modern transport system (including high-speed rail and others) for Belfast, with a cost of \xc2\xa3250&#160;million.<sup id="cite_ref-236" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-236">&#91;233&#93;</a></sup>\n</p><p>2017 was a great year for Belfast in terms of tourism with nearly 1.5&#160;million trips being made to the city, generating around 5&#160;million bed nights and incredible tourism revenue of 328&#160;million pounds.<sup id="cite_ref-237" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-237">&#91;234&#93;</a></sup>\n</p><p>In 2018, Belfast saw six new hotels being opened, with the biggest in Northern Ireland, the \xc2\xa353&#160;million <a href="/wiki/Grand_Central_Hotel_Belfast" title="Grand Central Hotel Belfast">Grand Central Hotel Belfast</a> officially open to the public. The other hotels included AC Marriot, Hampton By Hilton, EasyHotel, Maldron Belfast City Centre and Flint. The new hotels have helped to increase a further 1,000 bedrooms in the city.<sup id="cite_ref-auto_238-0" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-auto-238">&#91;235&#93;</a></sup>\nBelfast was successful in attracting many conferencing events, both national and international, to the city in 2018. Over 60 conferences took place that year with 30,000 people helping contribute to a record 45&#160;million pounds for the local economy.<sup id="cite_ref-auto_238-1" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-auto-238">&#91;235&#93;</a></sup>\n</p><p>There is a tourist information centre located at <a href="/wiki/Donegall_Square" title="Donegall Square">Donegall Square North</a>.<sup id="cite_ref-239" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-239">&#91;236&#93;</a></sup>\n</p>\n<h2><span id="Twin_towns_.E2.80.93_sister_cities"></span><span class="mw-headline" id="Twin_towns_\xe2\x80\x93_sister_cities">Twin towns \xe2\x80\x93 sister cities</span><span class="mw-editsection"><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">[</span><a href="/w/index.php?title=Belfast&amp;action=edit&amp;section=31" title="Edit section: Twin towns \xe2\x80\x93 sister cities">edit</a><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">]</span></span></h2>\n<p>Belfast City Council takes part in the <a href="/wiki/Twin_towns_and_sister_cities" class="mw-redirect" title="Twin towns and sister cities">twinning scheme</a>,<sup id="cite_ref-2014_cities_240-0" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-2014_cities-240">&#91;237&#93;</a></sup> and is twinned with the following sister cities:\n</p>\n<ul><li><a href="/wiki/Nashville" class="mw-redirect" title="Nashville">Nashville</a>, <a href="/wiki/Tennessee" title="Tennessee">Tennessee</a>, United States (since 1994)<sup id="cite_ref-2014_cities_240-1" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-2014_cities-240">&#91;237&#93;</a></sup></li>\n<li><a href="/wiki/Hefei" title="Hefei">Hefei</a>, <a href="/wiki/Anhui" title="Anhui">Anhui Province</a>, China (since 2005)<sup id="cite_ref-2014_cities_240-2" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-2014_cities-240">&#91;237&#93;</a></sup></li>\n<li><a href="/wiki/Boston" title="Boston">Boston</a>, <a href="/wiki/Massachusetts" title="Massachusetts">Massachusetts</a>, United States (since 2014)<sup id="cite_ref-2014_cities_240-3" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-2014_cities-240">&#91;237&#93;</a></sup></li>\n<li><a href="/wiki/Shenyang" title="Shenyang">Shenyang</a>, <a href="/wiki/Liaoning" title="Liaoning">Liaoning Province</a>, China (since 2016)<sup id="cite_ref-241" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-241">&#91;238&#93;</a></sup></li></ul>\n<h2><span class="mw-headline" id="Freedom_of_the_City">Freedom of the City</span><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">]</span></span></h2>\n<p>The following people and military units have received the <a href="/wiki/Freedom_of_the_City" title="Freedom of the City">Freedom of the City</a> of Belfast.\n</p>\n<div role="note" class="hatnote navigation-not-searchable plainlinks">This list is <a href="/wiki/Wikipedia:WikiProject_Lists#Incomplete_lists" title="Wikipedia:WikiProject
